reuelation iesus christ god gaue vnto end might shew seruaūtes thinges shoulde shortly come passe vsuall amonge prophet least shold thought spread abroad among commun people deuises owne brayne ascite god aucthor doctrine sorte word lord burthē word lord c selfe doth sainct iohn saying reuelatiō iesus christ sauing simplie alleage god onely aucthor apostle sheweth iesus christ haue deliuered thing vnto himselfe receiued father truely sainct iohn nourished vp cleare light gospell doth speake muche playnly sensibly vnto v thē prophet brought vp vnder shadowes moses law although christ eternall wisdome father alwaies prerogatiue deliuer forth heauenly oracle whose benefite wee ought knowledge selues haue receiued whatsoeuer good gift god hath time bestowed vpon church yet notwithstandinge manifest father time past vnder law yt sone god tooke flesh manifested selfe beholden v vnder ye clere light ye gospell ye vail taken away rightly therefore sayeth iohn reuelation iesus christ whereby doth onely seuer distinguish heauenly doctrine deuises men also extolleth great excellent dignitie sauioure iesus christ whome doth attribute diuine reuelatiō one say oure fleshe lifted vp exalted great honour euē made partaker god misteries ought seme straung christ placed right hand god father steed doth gouerne church moreouer whole world god gaue vnto might shew seruauntes c wonderfull goodnesse god doth shine forth vnto v doth vouchsafe reuels church great misteries secretes thinges come neither doth suffer seruauntes ignorant thing way profitable knowe therefore god appointed declared aucthor doctrine iesus christ whose meanes great treasure come vnto v mediator truely head god doth also imbrace v bodie refuse seruaunts readie receyue obey commaundements moreouer iohn meaneth woordes secretes onely knowne sauiour christ declared booke seing wisedome god part diuine counsaile hid vnderstandeth christ persone mediator hath receyued reuelatiō father might communicate church doubted god reuealed also manie thinges vision apostle holy men make eyther confirmatiō strengthninge el admonicion churche present would haue reuelation onely cōmitted writing ye vse whole church like cōming christ doctrine teaching darke obscure church stode nede many reuelations ye light gospell sprong vp hath dispersed driuen awaie cloudes darkenesse ought holde selues contente verie extraordinarie vision one therefore yet excellent reuelatiō holy ghost thought sufficient church might admonish peril • nd daungers shold passe iohn sayeth god gaue reuelation christ might declare seruaunts thinges shold shortly come passe although executiō fulfilling many thinges fore told booke differred vnto long time yet meaneth euen vtilitie profite prophecy take place horrible persecutiōs stirred vp church romane emperours euen little begunne stirred vp nero domitian sending angell teacheth whose ministrie reuelation brought vnto
